# <a name="dimensions-and-measures-available-in-call-quality-dashboard"></a><span data-ttu-id="24c4b-103">通话质量仪表板中可用的维度和衡量指标</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-103">Dimensions and measures available in Call Quality Dashboard</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-104">呼叫质量仪表板 (CQD) 的 Microsoft 团队和 Skype 业务 online 使您能够获得见解进行业务服务使用的 Microsoft 团队和 Skype 的呼叫的质量。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-104">The Call Quality Dashboard (CQD) for Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business Online allows you to gain insights into the quality of calls made using Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="24c4b-105">本主题详细介绍了 CQD 提供的维度和衡量指标。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-105">This topic provides detailed information about the dimensions and measures exposed by CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="24c4b-106">若要了解有关 CQD 以及如何启用它的详细信息，请参阅[打开和使用的 Microsoft 团队和 Skype 业务 online 呼叫质量仪表板](turning-on-and-using-call-quality-dashboard.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-106">To learn more about CQD and how to enable it, see [Turning on and using Call Quality Dashboard for Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business Online](turning-on-and-using-call-quality-dashboard.md).</span></span>

## <a name="first-and-second-endpoint-classification"></a><span data-ttu-id="24c4b-107">第一和第二终结点分类</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-107">First and Second endpoint classification</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-p102">通话质量仪表板 (CQD) 中的很多维度和衡量指标被标记为第一或第二。以下逻辑用于确定将流或通话中涉及的哪些终结点标为第一。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-p102">Many of the dimensions and measures in Call Quality Dashboard (CQD) are labeled as first or second. The following logic determines which endpoint involved in the stream or call is labeled as first:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="24c4b-110">首先将始终保持 （AV MCU、 中介服务器等） 中的服务器终结点如果流/呼叫中涉及的服务器。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-110">First will always be a Server endpoint (AV MCU, Mediation Server, etc.) if a Server is involved in the stream/call.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="24c4b-111">第二始终是指客户端终结点，除非流的两端均为服务器终结点。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-111">Second will always be a Client endpoint unless the stream is between two Server endpoints.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="24c4b-112">如果两个端点都相同的类型，其中的顺序是第一个与第二基于用户代理类别的内部排序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-112">If both endpoints are the same type, the order for which is first vs. second is based on internal ordering of the user agent category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="24c4b-113">这样可以确保排序的一致性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-113">This ensures the ordering is consistent.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-114">例如，每行表示流中涉及的一对用户代理：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-114">For example, each row represents a pair of User Agents involved in a stream:</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="24c4b-p104">[!注释] 第一和第二分类与终结点是呼叫方还是被叫方无关。"第一是呼叫方"维度可以用来帮助确定哪个终结点是呼叫方或被叫方。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-p104">That First and Second classification is separate from which endpoint is the caller or callee. The First Is Caller dimension can be used to help identify which endpoint was the caller or callee.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-157">下表列出了 CQD 中目前使用的维度：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-157">The following table lists the dimensions currently available in CQD:</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-158">**维度名称**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-158">**Dimension name**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-159">**数据类型/单位**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-159">**Data type / Units**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-160">**说明**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-160">**Description**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-161">**值**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-161">**Values**</span></span> <br/> |

|<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1645">Call Setup Failure Reason</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1645">Call Setup Failure Reason</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1646">枚举</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1646">Enumeration</span></span>  <br/> | <span data-ttu-id="24c4b-p265">通话未能建立媒体连接的原因分类。可能的值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-p265">Classification of why media connection could not be established for a call. This may be due to proxy or firewall rules not being correctly configured.</span></span> <br/>  <span data-ttu-id="24c4b-p267">缺少 FW IP 阻止免除规则 - 表示路径上的网络设备可能阻止与 Office 365 网络建立媒体路径。这可能是因为未正确将代理或防火墙规则配置为允许访问用于 Skype for Business 流量的 IP 地址和端口。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-p267">Missing FW IP Block Exemption Rule - indicates that network equipment along the path likely prevented the media path from being established to the Office 365 network. This may be due to proxy or firewall rules not being correctly configured to allow access to IP addresses and ports used for Skype for Business traffic.</span></span> <br/>  <span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1653">其他 - 表示通话无法建立媒体路径，但是未能对根本原因进行分类。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1653">Other - indicates the media path for the call could not be established but the root cause could not be classified.</span></span> <br/>  <span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1654">不媒体失败-指示使用的媒体路径建立检测到没有问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1654">Not Media Failure - indicates no issue was detected with the establishment of the media path.</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1655">空值表示通话没有因为已知的媒体问题而未能建立。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1655">Blank values indicate call set up did not fail due to a known media issue.</span></span>  <br/><span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1656">**示例值：** 缺少 FW IP 阻止免除规则</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1656">**Example value:** Missing FW IP Block Exemption Rule</span></span>  <br/> |

### <a name="notes-on-dimension-data-typeunits"></a><span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1764">关于维度数据类型/单位的说明：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1764">Notes on dimension data type/units:</span></span>

#### <a name="range"></a><span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1765">范围</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1765">Range</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1766">按范围或分组表示的维度值使用以下格式显示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1766">Dimensions that are provided as range or group of values are shown using the following format:</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1767">_\<排序顺序字符串\>[\<下限非独占\> - \<上限独占\>)_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1767">_\<sort order string\> [\<lower bound inclusive\> - \<upper bound exclusive\>)_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1768">例如，持续时间（分钟）维度表示以分钟为单位的通话持续时间，报告的值以取值范围的形式表示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1768">For example, the Duration (Minutes) dimension represents the call duration in seconds with the value reported as a range of values.</span></span>

|||
|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1769">**Duration (Minutes)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1769">**Duration (Minutes)**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1770">**解释方法**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1770">**How to interpret**</span></span> <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1771">062: [0 - 0)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1771">062: [0 - 0)</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1772">流持续时间 = 0 分钟</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1772">Stream duration = 0 minutes</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1773">064: [1 - 2)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1773">064: [1 - 2)</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1774">1 分钟 < = 流持续时间 < 2 分钟</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1774">1 minute < = stream duration < 2 minutes</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1775">065: [2 - 3)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1775">065: [2 - 3)</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1776">2 分钟 < = 流持续时间 < 3 分钟</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1776">2 minutes < = stream duration < 3 minutes</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1777">066: [3 - 4)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1777">066: [3 - 4)</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1778">3 分钟 < = 流持续时间 < 4 分钟</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1778">3 minutes < = stream duration < 4 minutes</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1779">…</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1779"></span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1780">…</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1780"></span></span>  <br/> |

<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-p275"><排序字符串> 用于控制数据显示的顺序，可以用于筛选功能。例如，利用持续时间（分钟）<"065"的筛选器可以显示持续时间小于 2 分钟的流（筛选器应包含前导"0"才能正常使用）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-p275">The <sort order string> is used to control the sort order when presenting the data and can be used for filtering. For example, a filter on Duration (Minutes) < "065", would show streams with duration less than 2 minutes (The leading '0' is needed for the filter to work as expected).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1783">[!注释] 排序字符串的实际值并不重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1783">The actual value of the sort order string isn't significant.</span></span>

#### <a name="enumeration-pair"></a><span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1784">枚举对</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1784">Enumeration pair</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1785">按枚举对表示的维度使用以下格式显示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1785">Dimensions that are provided as an enumeration pair are shown using the following format:</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1786">_\<从一个终结点的枚举值\>:\<从其他终结点的枚举值\>_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1786">_\<enumeration value from one end point\> : \<enumeration value from the other endpoint\>_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1787">枚举值的顺序一致，但此顺序不反映第一或第二终结点的顺序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1787">The ordering of the enumeration values is consistent but doesn't reflect ordering of the first or second endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1788">例如，网络连接详情对显示两个终结点的网络连接详情值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1788">For example, the Network Connection Detail Pair shows the Network Connection Detail values for the two endpoints:</span></span>

|||
|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1789">**Network Connection Detail Pair**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1789">**Network Connection Detail Pair**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1790">**解释方法**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1790">**How to interpret**</span></span> <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1791">有线 : 有线</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1791">Wired : Wired</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1792">第一和第二终结点均使用有线以太网连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1792">First and second endpoints both used wired ethernet connections.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1793">有线 : wifi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1793">Wired : wifi</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1794">第一个终结点使用有线以太网连接且第二个终结点使用 Wi-Fi 连接，或第二个终结点使用有线以太网连接且第一个终结点使用 Wi-Fi 连接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1794">First endpoint used wired ethernet connection and second endpoint used Wi-Fi connection, or the second endpoint used wired ethernet connection and first endpoint used Wi-Fi connection.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1795">: wifi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1795">: wifi</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1796">第一个终结点使用 WiFi 连接且第二个终结点使用的网络连接未知，或第二个终结点使用 WiFi 连接且第一个终结点使用的网络连接未知。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1796">First endpoint used a WiFi connection and the network connection used by the second endpoint is unknown, or the second endpoint used a WiFi connection and the network connection used by the first endpoint is unknown.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1797">…</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1797"></span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1798">…</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1798"></span></span>  <br/> |

#### <a name="blank-values"></a><span data-ttu-id="24c4b-1799">空值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-1799">Blank values</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="24c4b-p276">上表列出了维度可能出现空值的原因。如果"QoE 记录可用性"维度为 False，则很多维度和衡量指标都将为空。这通常出现在通话未能成功建立的情况下。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="24c4b-p276">The table above lists possible reasons why a dimension may be blank. Many dimensions and measures will be blank if the QoE Record Available dimension is false. This typically occurs when the call wasn't successfully established.</span></span>
